	SPR_move_capital_to_lacoruna = {
		allowed = {
			tag = SPR	
		}

		icon = generic_nationalism
		priority = -1
		available = {
			SPR = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = SPR_move_capital
				}
				controls_state = 171
			}
		}
		days_re_enable = 60
		cost = 0
		visible = {
			SPR = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = SPR_move_capital
				}
			}
			has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war
			NOT = {
				has_global_flag = scw_over
				282 = {
					has_state_flag = no_china_war_state_flag
					has_state_flag = no_partial_china_war_state_flag
				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_capital = {state=171}
			set_country_flag = { flag = SPR_move_capital value = 1 days = 60 }
		}	
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 0
		}
	}

SPR_the_inevitable_civil_war = {
	SPA_carlist_uprising_mission = {
		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		allowed = {
			tag = SPA
		}

		available = {
			always = no
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		priority = 10

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_mission_timeout = 526

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPA
			  
			is_ai = no							   
			always = no
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_controlled_states > 4
				}
				country_event = lar_spain.7
			}
			else = {
				activate_mission = SPA_carlist_uprising_mission
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = SPA_carlist_uprising_mission
					days = -526
				}
			}
		}
	}

	SPR_anarchist_uprising_mission = {

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		allowed = {
			tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
			always = no
		}

		priority = 10

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_mission_timeout = 246

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			is_ai = no	 
			tag = SPD
									   
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = SPR_crush_the_revolution }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_controlled_states > 1
				}
				country_event = lar_spain.9
			}
			else = {
				activate_mission = SPR_anarchist_uprising_mission
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = SPR_anarchist_uprising_mission
					days = -211
				}
			}
		}
	}

	SPR_surrender_button = {

		priority = 1

		icon = generic_ignite_civil_war

		available = {
			has_war = yes
			surrender_progress > 0.6
			date > 1938.1.1
		}


		fire_only_once = yes


		visible = {
			tag = SPR
			has_war = yes
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_global_flag = SPR_has_surrendered_flag
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = SPA_death_before_surrender
				add_idea = SPA_death_before_surrender2
			}
		}
	}

	

	SPR_imprison_primo_de_rivera = {

		icon = generic_independence

		allowed = {
			tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_primo_de_rivera_first_speech
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SPA_primo_de_rivera_imprisoned
				has_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
			}
		}

		cost = 15

		fire_only_once = yes

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 200
		}

		days_remove = 37

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPR
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_political_power = 25
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPA_military_plot_nationalists
				days = -35
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
			set_country_flag = SPA_primo_de_rivera_imprisoned
			custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_imprison_primo_de_rivera_tt
		}

	}

	SPR_secure_leader_loyalty = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		allowed = {
			tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
			}
			any_army_leader = {
				has_unit_leader_flag = SPA_swayed_leader_loyalty_flag
			}
		}

		cost = 30

		fire_only_once = no

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 200
		}

		days_remove = 37

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPR
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_military_plot_republicans
				days = 37
			}
			random_unit_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = trait_SPA_nationalist_sympathies
					has_unit_leader_flag = SPA_swayed_leader_loyalty_flag
				}
				remove_unit_leader_trait = trait_SPA_nationalist_sympathies
				clr_unit_leader_flag = SPA_swayed_leader_loyalty_flag
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

	}

	SPR_reassign_disloyal_leader = {

		icon = generic_army_support

		allowed = {
			tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
			}
			any_army_leader = {
				has_trait = trait_SPA_nationalist_sympathies
			}
		}

		cost = 30

		fire_only_once = no

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 200
		}

		days_remove = 37

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPR
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_military_plot_republicans
				days = 37
			}
			random_army_leader = {
				limit = {
					has_trait = trait_SPA_nationalist_sympathies
					NOT = {
						has_unit_leader_flag = SPA_swayed_leader_loyalty_flag
						has_unit_leader_flag = SPR_reassigned_flag
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_reassign_disloyal_leader_tt
				set_unit_leader_flag = SPR_reassigned_flag # Generates trait upon SCW start that makes them useless for 60 days.
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

	}

	SPA_suppress_the_strikes = {

		icon = oppression

		allowed = {
			OR = {
				tag = SPR
			 
			}
		}

		available = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
			}
			NOT = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SPA_suppress_the_strikes_tt
					has_idea = SPR_national_strikes_1
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 30

		fire_only_once = no

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 200
		}

		days_remove = 37

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			OR = {
				tag = SPR
			 
			}
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPA_military_plot_nationalists
				days = -35
			}
			SPN = {
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = SPR_military_plot_republicans
					days = -35
				}
			}
			SPR_suppress_the_strikes_increase = yes
			clr_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

	}

				has_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag

			NOT = {
				custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SPA_suppress_the_strikes_tt
					has_idea = SPR_national_strikes_9
				}
			}
		}

		cost = 20

		fire_only_once = no

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 500
		}

		days_remove = 37

		modifier = {
			
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPN
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}
		

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

		remove_effect = {
			SPR = {
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = SPA_military_plot_nationalists
					days = 30
				}
			}
			SPN = {
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = SPR_military_plot_republicans
					days = 30
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPR_inevitable_civil_war_in_progress_flag
		}

					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}

					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt

						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}

					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front

				171 = {

					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }

					}

					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				171 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_secure_the_northern_garrisons }
				factor = 0

				 state = 791 }}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 791.SPA_garrison_control_cost?10

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 10

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPN
				}
				SPR = {
					activate_mission = SPA_expand_influence_in_the_valladolid_garrison_mission
				}
				
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPR
				}
				SPN = {
					activate_mission = SPA_expand_influence_in_the_valladolid_garrison_mission
				}
				
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				791 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}

				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				791 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt

						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				791 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {

		highlight_states = {
 			highlight_state_targets = { 
				 state =172 }}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 172.SPA_garrison_control_cost?10

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 10

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPN
				}
				SPR = {
					activate_mission = SPA_expand_influence_in_the_navarra_garrison_mission
				}
				
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPR
				}
				SPN = {
					activate_mission = SPA_expand_influence_in_the_navarra_garrison_mission
				}
				
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				172 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				172 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				172 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				NOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_secure_the_northern_garrisons }
				factor = 0
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain

			}

 			highlight_state_targets = { 
				 state = 165 }}

		on_map_mode = map_only

		cost = 165.SPA_garrison_control_cost?10

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 10

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPN
				}
				SPR = {
					activate_mission = SPA_expand_influence_in_the_catalunya_garrison_mission
				}
				
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPR
				}
				SPN = {
					activate_mission = SPA_expand_influence_in_the_catalunya_garrison_mission
				}
				
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				165 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				165 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				165 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				165 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }

				is_historical_focus_on = yes
				factor = 0
			}
		}

							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				793 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				793 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				793 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain

		cost = 168.SPA_garrison_control_cost?10

		fire_only_once = no

		days_remove = 10

		visible = {
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
		}

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		complete_effect = {
			set_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPN
				}
				SPR = {
					activate_mission = SPA_expand_influence_in_the_murcia_garrison_mission
				}
				
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPR
				}
				SPN = {
					activate_mission = SPA_expand_influence_in_the_murcia_garrison_mission
				}
				
			}
		}

		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				168 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						if = {
							limit = { check_variable = { SPA_garrison_control < 4 } }
							
							add_to_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
							SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
							SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						}
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				168 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 15 }
					hidden_effect = {
						subtract_from_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 1 }
						SPR = { subtract_from_variable = { var = spa_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
						SPR = { add_to_variable = { var = spr_civil_war_divisions_counter_var value = 1 } }
					}
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = SPA_already_expanding_influence_flag
		}

		ai_will_do = {
			base = 110
			modifier = {
				168 = { has_state_flag = SPR_recently_expanded_influence_flag }
				factor = 10
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				168 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 2 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }
				factor = 5
			}
			modifier = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				168 = { check_variable = { var = SPA_garrison_control value = 3 compare = greater_than_or_equals } }

			}

	SPR_political_assassination_mission = {

		icon = spr_political_assassination

		allowed = {
			tag = SPN
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 36

		is_good = yes

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			SPR = {
				has_decision = SPA_political_assassination
			}
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPN
			SPR = {
				has_decision = SPA_political_assassination
			}

	SPA_expand_influence_in_the_galicia_garrison_mission = {

		icon = generic_prepare_civil_war

		allowed = {
			tag = SPR
		}

		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		highlight_states = {
 			highlight_state_targets = { 
				 state = 171 }}

		on_map_mode = map_and_decisions_view

		fire_only_once = no

		days_mission_timeout = 9

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPR
			has_country_flag = SPR_spanish_elections_flag
			NOT = { has_global_flag = spanish_civil_war }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			171 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain }
				
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 10 }
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front }
					}
					set_state_flag = { flag = SPR_ai_recently_expanded_influence_flag value = 1 days = 10 }
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_the_popular_front
				}
				171 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPA_expand_influence_nationalists_tt
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
				}
			
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_completed_focus = SPA_a_great_spain
				}
				171 = {
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_expand_influence_republicans_tt
					SPA_garrison_control_tooltip = yes
					SPA_garrison_control_cost_calculation = yes
				}
				
			}
		}

	}

		allowed = {

		}

			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
		}

		priority = 10

		fire_only_once = yes

		days_mission_timeout = SPR_communists_uprising_mission_var?246

		is_good = no

		cancel_if_not_visible = yes

		activation = {
			always = no
		}

		visible = {
			tag = SPD
									   
			NOT = { has_completed_focus = SPR_masters_of_our_own_fate }
		}

		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					num_of_controlled_states > 1
				}
				country_event = lar_spain.10
			}
			else = {
				activate_mission = SPR_government_crackdown_mission
				add_days_mission_timeout = {
					mission = SPR_government_crackdown_mission
					days = -211
				}
			}
		}
	}

	SPR_plan_state_marking_check_1 = {
 		icon = generic_industry
 		available = {
			hidden_trigger = { always = no }
 		}
		visible = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					phase_one_max_states_var > 8
				}
			}	
		}
		activation = {
			SPR = {
				has_completed_focus = SPA_supercharge_the_War_economy
			}
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					phase_one_max_states_var > 8
				}
			}
		} 
		fixed_random_seed = no
		is_good = no
		fire_only_once = no
 		days_mission_timeout = 1
		days_remove = 2
		timeout_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					SPR = {
						has_completed_focus = SPA_supercharge_the_War_economy
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
						phase_one_max_states_var >	8
						}
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					activate_mission = SPR_plan_state_marking_check_1			
				}
			}	
			SPR = {
				random_owned_state = {
					limit = {
						NOT  = {
						state = 178
						state = 699
						state = 297
						state = 290
						state = 177
						state = 783
						}
						NOT = {
							has_state_flag = SPR_DEV_PLAN_IC
						}
					}
					set_state_flag = SPR_DEV_PLAN_IC
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_focus_dev_plan_mark_1
					custom_override_tooltip = {
						tooltip = potential_outcome_right_1
							random_list = {
							3 = {
								
							}
							4 = {
								add_to_variable = {
									SPR_RIGHT_industry_consumer_goods_factor = 0.001
									tooltip = consumer_goods_tooltip
								}
							}
							3 = {
								add_to_variable = {
									SPR_RIGHT_industry_consumer_goods_factor = 0.002
									tooltip = consumer_goods_tooltip
								}
							}
						}
					}

					custom_effect_tooltip = MANspace
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_custom_mill_1_tooltip_mission
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_first_phase_second_dev
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_progress_dev_plan_1
				}
				add_to_variable = { var = SPR_1_dev_plan value = 1 }
				add_to_variable = {
					var = phase_one_max_states_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		cancel_trigger = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_economic_colapse
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
					tooltip = SPR_state_marked_max_tooltip
					check_variable = {
						phase_one_max_states_var < 9
					}
			}
		}
 	}

								has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_1
								has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_3
							}
						}
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
						add_building_construction = {
							type = infrastructure
							level = 1
						}
					}
					add_stability = -0.01
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						any_state = {
							NOT = {
								has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_1
								has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_2
								has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_3
							}
						}
					}
					random_owned_state = {
						add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
						add_building_construction = {
							type = infrastructure
							level = 1
						}
					}
					add_stability = -0.03
				}
			}

		if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_flag = infrastructure_mission
				}
				add_to_variable = {
					var  = industrial_points
					value = 2
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = MANspace
				custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_industrial_points_2
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						or = {
							has_country_flag = industrial_mission
							has_country_flag = resources_mission
						}
						
					}
					add_to_variable = {
						var  = industrial_points
						value = 1
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = MANspace
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_industrial_points_1
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_flag = infrastructure_mission
							has_country_flag = industrial_mission
							has_country_flag = resources_mission
						}
					}
					custom_effect_tooltip = MANspace
					custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_no_points
				}
			}

		}
	}

	##### actual missions careful with em #####
	SPR_industrial_mission = {
		icon = generic_construction

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = industrial_points_needed_4
					
				check_variable = {
					var = industrial_points
					value > 3
				}
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = industrial_mission
			any_state = {
				has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_1
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			always = no
		}
		
		days_mission_timeout = 180 #180
		days_remove = 1 #1

		timeout_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_eco_modif
			add_to_variable = {
				var = SPR_LEFT_industry_production_speed_industrial_complex_factor
				value = -0.025
				tooltip = industrial_complex_build_speed_factor_tooltip
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			add_stability = -0.05

			clr_country_flag = moderate_wing_request
			clr_country_flag = industrial_mission
			SPR = {
					activate_mission = SPR_parlament_meeting
			}
			every_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_1
					}
					
					clr_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_1

				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_1
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = industrial_complex
					level = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				industrial_points = 0
			}
		}

		

		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_eco_modif
			add_to_variable = {
				var = SPR_LEFT_industry_production_speed_industrial_complex_factor
				value = 0.05
				tooltip = industrial_complex_build_speed_factor_tooltip
			}

			clr_country_flag = moderate_wing_request
			clr_country_flag = industrial_mission
			SPR = {
					activate_mission = SPR_parlament_meeting
			}
			every_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_1
					}
					
					clr_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_1

				}
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_parlament_meeting
				days = -180
			}
		}
	}

		timeout_effect = {
			army_experience = -35
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.05

			clr_country_flag = radical_wing_request
			clr_country_flag = military_mission
			SPR = {
					activate_mission = SPR_parlament_meeting
			}
			every_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_5
					}
					
					clr_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_5

				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_5
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = arms_factory
					level = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				military_points = 0
			}
		}

		

		remove_effect = {

			custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_eco_modif
			add_to_variable = {
				var = SPR_LEFT_industry_production_speed_arms_factory_factor
				value = 0.025
				tooltip = arms_factory_build_speed_factor_tooltip
			}

			clr_country_flag = radical_wing_request
			clr_country_flag = military_mission
			SPR = {
					activate_mission = SPR_parlament_meeting
			}
			every_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_5
					}
					
					clr_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_5

				}
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_parlament_meeting
				days = -180
			}
		}
	}

	SPR_dockyards_mission = {
		icon = GFX_decision_generic_merge_plant_materiel

		available = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = military_points_needed_4
					
				check_variable = {
					var = military_points
					value > 3
				}
			}
		}
		is_good = no
		activation = {
			has_country_flag = dockyard_mission
			any_state = {
				has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_6
			}
		}
		
		visible = {
			always = no
		}
		
		days_mission_timeout = 180 #180
		days_remove = 1 #1

		timeout_effect = {
			army_experience = -35
			add_stability = -0.05
			add_war_support = -0.05

			clr_country_flag = radical_wing_request
			clr_country_flag = dockyard_mission
			SPR = {
					activate_mission = SPR_parlament_meeting
			}
			every_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_6
					}
					
					clr_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_6

				}
			}
		}

		complete_effect = {
			random_owned_state = {
				limit = {
					has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_6
					is_coastal = yes
				}
				add_building_construction = {
					type = dockyard
					level = 1
				}
			}
			set_variable = {
				military_points = 0
			}
		}

		

		remove_effect = {

			custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_eco_modif
			add_to_variable = {
				var = SPR_LEFT_industry_production_speed_dockyard_factor
				value = 0.025
				tooltip = arms_factory_build_speed_factor_tooltip
			}

			clr_country_flag = radical_wing_request
			clr_country_flag = dockyard_mission
			SPR = {
					activate_mission = SPR_parlament_meeting
			}
			every_state = {
				if = {
					limit = { 
						has_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_6
					}
					
					clr_state_flag = DEVELOPMENT_PROGRAM_6

				}
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = SPR_parlament_meeting
				days = -180
			}
		}
	}
